Abstract: Reasoning LLMs-as-Judges, which can benefit from inference-time scaling, provide a promising path for extending the success of reasoning models to non-verifiable domains where the output correctness/quality cannot be directly checked. However, while reasoning judges have shown better performance on static evaluation benchmarks, their effectiveness in actual policy training has not been systematically examined. Therefore, we conduct a rigorous study to investigate the actual impact of non-reasoning and reasoning judges in reinforcement-learning-based LLM alignment. Our controlled synthetic setting, where a "gold-standard" judge (gpt-oss-120b) provides preference annotations to train smaller judges, reveals key differences between non-reasoning and reasoning judges: non-reasoning judges lead to reward hacking easily, while reasoning judges can lead to policies that achieve strong performance when evaluated by the gold-standard judge. Interestingly, we find that the reasoning-judge-trained policies achieve such strong performance by learning to generate highly effective adversarial outputs that can also score well on popular benchmarks such as Arena-Hard by deceiving other LLM-judges. Combined with our further analysis, our study highlights both important findings and room for improvements for applying (reasoning) LLM-judges in non-verifiable LLM post-training.

</details>


### [181] [Compiling Temporal Numeric Planning into Discrete PDDL+: Extended Version](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12188)
*Andrea Micheli,Enrico Scala,Alessandro Valentini*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 将带有持续动作的时态规划编译为PDDL+的实用方法


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然PDDL+语言引入时就知道时态规划可以编译到PDDL+，但文献中一直缺乏实用的编译方法。本文旨在填补这一空白，提供实用的编译方案。

Method: 提出从带有持续动作的时态规划到PDDL+的多项式时间编译方法，完全捕获语义，仅假设动作不自我重叠。编译保持规划长度在常数因子内。

Result: 实验证明该方法对困难的时态数值问题具有实际应用价值，编译是多项式复杂度的，且规划长度仅增加常数倍。

Conclusion: 首次提供了实用的时态规划到PDDL+的编译方法，为处理困难的时态数值规划问题提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Since the introduction of the PDDL+ modeling language, it was known that temporal planning with durative actions (as in PDDL 2.1) could be compiled into PDDL+. However, no practical compilation was presented in the literature ever since. We present a practical compilation from temporal planning with durative actions into PDDL+, fully capturing the semantics and only assuming the non-self-overlapping of actions. Our compilation is polynomial, retains the plan length up to a constant factor and is experimentally shown to be of practical relevance for hard temporal numeric problems.

</details>


### [182] [Portfolio of Solving Strategies in CEGAR-based Object Packing and Scheduling for Sequential 3D Printing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12224)
*Pavel Surynek*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 并行化CEGAR-SEQ算法用于3D打印对象排列与调度，通过组合多种对象排列策略的Portfolio-CEGAR-SEQ在性能上超越原算法


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代多核个人计算机CPU具备强大的并行计算能力，可用于解决复杂的组合优化问题。研究旨在利用这些计算资源改进3D打印中的对象排列和调度问题

Method: 提出Portfolio-CEGAR-SEQ算法：1) 并行执行CEGAR-SEQ算法；2) 采用多种对象排列策略组合（包括原中心放置策略、角落放置策略、按高度调度策略）；3) 将问题表达为线性算术公式，采用基于反例引导抽象精化(CEGAR)的技术求解

Result: Portfolio-CEGAR-SEQ在性能上优于原始CEGAR-SEQ算法。在批量对象多打印板调度场景中，Portfolio-CEGAR-SEQ通常使用更少的打印板

Conclusion: 通过并行化CEGAR-SEQ算法并采用多种对象排列策略组合，能够有效利用现代多核CPU的计算能力，显著提升3D打印对象排列和调度问题的求解效率

Abstract: Computing power that used to be available only in supercomputers decades ago especially their parallelism is currently available in standard personal computer CPUs even in CPUs for mobile telephones. We show how to effectively utilize the computing power of modern multi-core personal computer CPU to solve the complex combinatorial problem of object arrangement and scheduling for sequential 3D printing. We achieved this by parallelizing the existing CEGAR-SEQ algorithm that solves the sequential object arrangement and scheduling by expressing it as a linear arithmetic formula which is then solved by a technique inspired by counterexample guided abstraction refinement (CEGAR). The original CEGAR-SEQ algorithm uses an object arrangement strategy that places objects towards the center of the printing plate. We propose alternative object arrangement strategies such as placing objects towards a corner of the printing plate and scheduling objects according to their height. Our parallelization is done at the high-level where we execute the CEGAR-SEQ algorithm in parallel with a portfolio of object arrangement strategies, an algorithm is called Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ. Our experimental evaluation indicates that Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ outperforms the original CEGAR-SEQ. When a batch of objects for multiple printing plates is scheduled, Portfolio-CEGAR-SEQ often uses fewer printing plates than CEGAR-SEQ.

</details>

### [183] [Strict Optimality of Frequency Estimation Under Local Differential Privacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11523)
*Mingen Pan*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文证明了在本地差分隐私下频率估计的严格最优精度，提出了具有对称极值配置和优化支撑大小的最优估计器，其通信成本可低至log₂(d(d-1)/2+1)，并展示了改进的Count-Mean Sketch在实际中接近理论最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究本地差分隐私(LDP)下频率估计的最优精度问题，旨在建立理论最优性界限并提供实际部署的选择指南。

Method: 1. 证明具有对称极值配置和恒定优化支撑大小的频率估计器能达到最大精度；2. 推导最优估计器的最小通信成本公式；3. 提出生成最优估计器的算法；4. 引入改进的Count-Mean Sketch方法；5. 与现有方法进行理论比较。

Result: 1. 建立了LDP频率估计的严格最优精度界限；2. 最优估计器通信成本可低至log₂(d(d-1)/2+1)，其中d为字典大小；3. 改进的Count-Mean Sketch在字典足够大时(如d=100, ε=1)与理论最优性几乎无法区分；4. 实验验证了理论推导的正确性。

Conclusion: 本文为LDP频率估计提供了严格的最优性理论框架，证明了对称极值配置估计器的最优性，推导了最小通信成本，提出的改进Count-Mean Sketch在实际应用中接近理论最优，为实际部署提供了选择指南。

Abstract: This paper establishes the strict optimality in precision for frequency estimation under local differential privacy (LDP). We prove that a frequency estimator with a symmetric and extremal configuration, and a constant support size equal to an optimized value, is sufficient to achieve maximum precision. Furthermore, we derive that the communication cost of such an optimal estimator can be as low as $\log_2(\frac{d(d-1)}{2}+1)$, where $d$ denotes the dictionary size, and propose an algorithm to generate this optimal estimator.
  In addition, we introduce a modified Count-Mean Sketch and demonstrate that it is practically indistinguishable from theoretical optimality with a sufficiently large dictionary size (e.g., $d=100$ for a privacy factor of $ε= 1$). We compare existing methods with our proposed optimal estimator to provide selection guidelines for practical deployment. Finally, the performance of these estimators is evaluated experimentally, showing that the empirical results are consistent with our theoretical derivations.

</details>


### [184] [Duality and decoding of linearized Algebraic Geometry codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11826)
*Elena Berardini,Xavier Caruso,Fabrice Drain*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出多项式时间解码算法用于线性化代数几何码，该算法适用于未分支求值点的线性化代数几何码，这是一类在函数域上除代数上的和秩度量求值码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究线性化代数几何码的解码问题，这类码在除代数上的和秩度量中具有应用价值。需要为这类特殊结构的编码设计高效解码算法。

Method: 通过建立除代数的Serre对偶性和Riemann-Roch定理，证明线性化代数几何码的对偶码（称为线性化微分码）在伴随代数上与线性化代数几何码重合，并基于此设计多项式时间解码算法。

Result: 成功设计出多项式时间解码算法，并证明其正确性。建立了线性化代数几何码与线性化微分码之间的对偶关系，为解码提供了理论基础。

Conclusion: 该工作为线性化代数几何码提供了有效的解码方案，通过建立除代数上的对偶理论，证明了算法的正确性，扩展了代数几何码在除代数和秩度量中的应用。

Abstract: We design a polynomial time decoding algorithm for linearized Algebraic Geometry codes with unramified evaluation places, a family of sum-rank metric evaluation codes on division algebras over function fields. By establishing a Serre duality and a Riemann-Roch theorem for these algebras, we prove that the dual codes of such linearized Algebraic Geometry codes, that we term linearized Differential codes, coincide with the linearized Algebraic Geometry codes themselves over the adjoint algebra, and that our decoding algorithm is correct.

</details>
